     edit
     Publish Center Redesign + Template System

     Context

     The user wants the Publish Center reimagined around a multi-profile,
     AI-assisted publishing flow with reusable templates. The current
     PublishCenter.vue (1,665 lines) is a multi-tab UI that supports either a
     single profile or a legacy platform per tab вҖ” it does not match the desired
      UX (multi-profile selection, per-account editable AI drafts,
     single-media-platform auto-stagger, screenshots-from-video,
     save-as-template). Crucially, the heavy backend infrastructure already
     exists: profile-scoped AI services + system prompt, per-platform character
     limits, watermark for video and image (4 styles), intro/outro concat, audio
      transcription, job queue with per-target schedule_at, and a firstComment
     field already populated by the LLM. The work is mostly (a) filling the gaps
      (screenshots, per-account regeneration with account context, stagger
     orchestration, link-in-first-comment uploader support, templates) and (b)
     replacing the UI to drive that capability.

     The user explicitly answered:
     1. Single-media platforms with multiple uploaded files вҶ’ split into N 
     posts, 5 minutes apart.
     2. Replace PublishCenter.vue entirely.
     3. AI rewrite is per-platform by default with a per-account "Regenerate" 
     button; honor a "Platform specification" section in the profile's system
     prompt that specifies per-account or per-platform rules; user can edit
     drafts.
     4. Templates save everything by default with per-setting deselect 
     checkboxes; add a new sidebar entry "Template Management".

     The deployment is Docker Compose (docker-compose.yml at repo root, single
     social-auto-upload service on port 5409). Final deliverable is rebuilt
     image + green end-to-end smoke test + push to GitHub.

     High-Level Architecture

     ---
     Backend Changes

     1. Screenshot extraction utility вҖ” myUtils/media_pipeline.py

     Add a new function alongside extract_video_audio():

     def extract_video_screenshots(
         source_path, output_dir, *, count, timestamps=None, seed=0,
         name_template="{stem}_{date}_screenshot{n}.jpg", runner=run_subprocess,
         duration_reader=probe_video_duration,
     ) -> list[Path]

     - If timestamps is None вҶ’ generate count evenly-spaced offsets across the
     video duration with a small random jitter (deterministic via seed).
     - If timestamps is a list of seconds (floats) or HH:MM:SS strings вҶ’ parse
     and use directly.
     - Naming: {originalname}_{YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS}_screenshot{N}.jpg (date stamp at
      extraction time).
     - Implementation: one ffmpeg -ss {t} -i {src} -vframes 1 -q:v 2 {out} per
     shot. Use probe_video_duration for default random offsets.
     - Returns the list of output Path objects in order.

     2. Wire screenshots into the campaign pipeline вҖ” sau_backend.py

     In _prepare_campaign_media_artifacts() (sau_backend.py:2154):

     - Accept a new screenshots_spec field from request_data:
     {"enabled": true, "count": 3, "timestamps": null | [12.0, 45.0, ...]}
     - For each video media file, after watermarking, call
     media_pipeline.extract_video_screenshots(...) writing to the campaign
     workspace under screenshots/.
     - Save each shot as a campaign_artifacts row with
     artifact_kind="screenshot" so the UI can list them.
     - Optionally upload to remote storage when uploadToRemote is set (use
     existing rclone_storage.upload_artifact).
     - Surface the shot paths/URLs in the return dict
     (artifacts_context["screenshotPaths"] / ["screenshotUrls"]) so the preview
     endpoint can expose them.

     3. Per-account draft generation вҖ” sau_backend.py

     Add a new helper that wraps _generate_platform_draft:

     def _generate_account_draft(
         account: profile_registry.Account,
         profile: profile_registry.Profile,
         media_group, request_data, media_context,
         *, regenerate: bool = False,
     ) -> dict

     - Append account context to the user prompt produced by
     _build_generation_prompt:
       - Account name: {account.account_name}
       - Platform: {account.platform}
       - A literal instruction: "If the system prompt contains a 'Platform 
     specification' or 'Account specification' section with rules for this 
     account, follow them."
     - When regenerate=True, bump the temperature (e.g. 0.7) and pass a
     different seed/random suffix so the LLM produces variation.
     - The result still flows through content_rules.prepare_platform_draft(...)
     so char limits, hashtags, emoji rules are enforced.

     Important: the existing _generate_platform_draft already returns
     firstComment; surface that field in every per-account draft.

     4. Single-media platform support matrix вҖ” myUtils/platform_capabilities.py 
     (new)

     Centralize what each platform supports so the orchestrator can decide when
     to split-and-stagger and whether firstComment is honored natively.

     SINGLE_MEDIA_PLATFORMS = {"tencent", "tiktok", "youtube", "telegram",
     "discord"}
     SUPPORTS_FIRST_COMMENT = {"facebook", "instagram", "twitter", "reddit",
     "youtube"}

     def platform_supports_multi_media(platform: str) -> bool: ...
     def platform_supports_first_comment(platform: str) -> bool: ...

     Single source of truth вҖ” reused by orchestrator + UI hints.

     5. Publish-center orchestrator вҖ” myUtils/publish_orchestrator.py (new)

     def submit_publish(
         *,
         profile_ids: list[int],
         selected_account_ids: list[int] | None,  # None = all enabled
         media_file_paths: list[str],
         brief: str,
         options: dict,   # {watermark, intro, outro, link_in_comment, 
     screenshots}
         schedule: dict | None,  # {startAt, dailyTimes, videosPerDay, ...} or 
     None
         account_drafts: dict[int, dict],  # accountId вҶ’ edited draft (optional 
     override)
         db_path: Path,
     ) -> dict

     Algorithm:
     1. Create one media group (media_group_store.create_media_group) carrying
     all uploaded files.
     2. For each profile_id:
       - Resolve accounts (intersect with selected_account_ids).
       - Create a campaign via campaign_store.create_campaign linked to the
     media group.
       - Call _prepare_campaign_media_artifacts(campaign.id, profile, 
     media_files, request_data, ...) once вҖ” this applies watermark, intro/outro,
      screenshots, and (optionally) transcription. request_data is constructed
     from options.
       - Group accounts by platform.
       - For each platform:
           - Build a draft: prefer account_drafts[account_id] if user edited;
     otherwise call _generate_account_draft (cached per platform when no account
      override exists).
         - Decide media batching:
               - If platform_supports_multi_media(platform) OR len(media_files) 
     == 1 вҶ’ one campaign post (existing behavior, all media used).
           - Else вҶ’ N campaign posts, each pinned to one media file via a new
     campaign_posts.file_record_ids field (see migration 0010 below). Stagger
     their target schedule_at by 5 minutes.
       - For each post, when enqueueing JobSpec.targets, set schedule_at per
     target according to the schedule (base time + per-platform stagger). The
     existing publish_job_targets.schedule_at column already supports this.
     3. Return {"campaigns": [campaign_payload, ...], "jobs": [job_payload, 
     ...]}.

     The orchestrator centralizes the "5-minutes-apart" logic so the worker
     stays untouched.

     6. Database migration вҖ” 
     migrations/versions/0010_publish_templates_and_post_files.py

     Two changes in one revision (small surface area):

     def upgrade():
         # publish_templates table
         op.create_table(
             "publish_templates",
             sa.Column("id", sa.Integer, primary_key=True, autoincrement=True),
             sa.Column("name", sa.Text, nullable=False),
             sa.Column("slug", sa.Text, nullable=False, unique=True),
             sa.Column("description", sa.Text, server_default=""),
             sa.Column("config_json", sa.Text, nullable=False,
     server_default="{}"),
             sa.Column("included_settings_json", sa.Text, nullable=False,
     server_default='["profileIds","accountIds","watermark","intro","outro","lin
     kInFirstComment","screenshots","schedule"]'),
             sa.Column("created_at", sa.DateTime,
     server_default=sa.func.current_timestamp()),
             sa.Column("updated_at", sa.DateTime,
     server_default=sa.func.current_timestamp()),
         )
         # Allow campaign posts to pin themselves to a subset of media files
         op.add_column("campaign_posts", sa.Column("file_record_ids_json",
     sa.Text, nullable=True))

     Update myUtils/campaigns.py (campaign_store) to read/write
     file_record_ids_json. When None/empty, behavior is unchanged (all media
     used). When set, the worker resolves only those files.

     7. Worker honors per-post file subset вҖ” myUtils/worker.py + 
     myUtils/prepared_publishers.py

     In _run_prepared_campaign_upload(...) (and the cookie-based campaign upload
      path), when the campaign post has file_record_ids_json, filter the
     artifact list to those records before handing off to the platform
     publisher. This is a small, localized change вҖ” most upload paths already
     take a list of files/artifacts; we just pre-filter that list.

     8. First-comment honoring in uploaders

     Today draft["firstComment"] is generated and stored, but no uploader
     actually posts it. Extend the publishers in myUtils/prepared_publishers.py
     for the platforms in SUPPORTS_FIRST_COMMENT:

     - Facebook: after POST /{page-id}/feed returns the post id, call POST 
     /{post-id}/comments with the comment text.
     - Instagram: after publishing the media container, call POST 
     /{ig-media-id}/comments (requires instagram_manage_comments scope вҖ” already
      in scopes if ENABLE_COMMENTS is set; we'll just attempt and log if it
     fails).
     - Twitter: post a reply tweet in_reply_to_status_id of the original.
     - Reddit: post a top-level comment on the submission ID.
     - YouTube: leave as TODO/log-only вҖ” YouTube comments-via-API require an
     additional scope; for v1 we'll just append the link to the description
     fallback.

     Guard each with a try/except so a failed first-comment doesn't fail the
     whole publish вҖ” log to logs/jobs/job-<id>.log.

     In payload building (orchestrator + _generate_account_draft):
     - If options.linkInFirstComment is true AND
     platform_supports_first_comment(platform): copy the link out of the message
      body into payload["firstComment"].
     - If link-in-first-comment is true but platform does NOT support it: leave
     link in the message body (no behavior change).

     9. Publish-center API endpoints вҖ” sau_backend.py

     Add four endpoints (all auth-gated by existing _enforce_auth middleware):

     Method + Path: POST /publish-center/preview
     Body: {profileIds, selectedAccountIds, mediaFilePaths, brief, options, 
       schedule}
     Returns: {profiles: [{profileId, profileName, accounts: [{accountId, 
       accountName, platform, draft: {message, hashtags, firstComment, 
     charCount, 
       maxChars}, supportsFirstComment, supportsMultiMedia}]}]}
     в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
     Method + Path: POST /publish-center/regenerate
     Body: {profileId, accountId, brief, mediaFilePaths, options}
     Returns: {draft: {...}}
     в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
     Method + Path: POST /publish-center/submit
     Body: {profileIds, selectedAccountIds, mediaFilePaths, brief, options, 
       schedule, accountDrafts}
     Returns: {campaignIds, jobs} вҖ” delegates to
     publish_orchestrator.submit_publish
     в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
     Method + Path: GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE /publish-templates[/{id}]
     Body: {name, description, config, includedSettings}
     Returns: Standard CRUD

     preview does NOT run watermark/intro/outro/screenshots вҖ” it only generates
     drafts. Heavy media processing happens on submit. This keeps preview fast.

     submit is the only path that creates campaigns and enqueues jobs.

     ---
     Verification Plan

     1. Schema migration
       - python db/createTable.py (runs alembic upgrade head); verify
     publish_templates and campaign_posts.file_record_ids_json exist via sqlite3
      db/database.db ".schema publish_templates".
     2. Unit-ish backend smoke
       - python -c "from myUtils.media_pipeline import 
     extract_video_screenshots" (import check).
       - curl -X POST http://localhost:5409/publish-center/preview -H 
     "Authorization: Bearer $SAU_API_TOKENS" -d '{"profileIds":[1],"mediaFilePat
     hs":["/app/videoFile/test.mp4"],"brief":"hello","options":{}}' вҖ” expect
     drafts per account.
     3. Frontend build
       - cd sau_frontend && npm install && npm run build вҖ” must complete without
      errors. Run dev server (npm run dev) on 5173 and load /publish-center and
     /template-management.
     4. End-to-end manual test in browser
       - Upload 1 video + 1 image.
       - Pick 2 profiles, deselect one account in each.
       - Toggle watermark + intro + outro + link-in-comment + screenshots
     (countВ 2).
       - Write a brief, click "Generate previews".
       - Verify per-account drafts appear with correct char counts; click
     "Regenerate" on one account and see it change.
       - Pick a single-media platform target (e.g. Tencent) with 2 media files вҖ”
      confirm UI hint about "2 posts 5 min apart" appears.
       - Click "Publish now"; watch /jobs page to see the staggered targets.
       - Save settings as a template (deselect "schedule"). Reload Publish
     Center, pick the template, only schedule remains blank.
       - Edit a template via /template-management, delete it.
     5. Docker rebuild & deploy
       - docker compose build --no-cache social-auto-upload
       - docker compose up -d social-auto-upload
       - docker compose logs -f social-auto-upload вҖ” watch for alembic upgrade 
     head success and Flask startup.
       - Open the production UI and re-run the manual smoke test (stepsВ 4)
     end-to-end. Iterate on any errors that surface.
     6. Push to GitHub
       - Only after all manual smoke tests pass and image runs clean.
       - One commit (or two: backend + frontend) with descriptive message: feat:
      redesigned Publish Center with multi-profile + per-account AI drafts + 
     templates.
       - git push origin main.

     ---
     Risks & Mitigations

     - Long LLM latency on preview: per-account regeneration is sequential.
     Mitigate by generating per-platform first, reusing the per-platform draft
     as the initial value for each account on that platform, and only making a
     fresh LLM call on explicit "Regenerate".
     - Per-platform first-comment APIs differ: keep each adapter small and
     wrapped in try/except; failures log but don't fail the publish.
     - Migration of campaign_posts adds a column on a table that's actively 
     used: SQLite tolerates ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN without a rewrite; the column
      is nullable and old rows behave identically.
     - Docker rebuild time: chromium reinstall is slow. Use layered caching;
     only --no-cache when needed for first verification.
     - Frontend bundle size: new view adds <50KB minified вҖ” no concern.

  rebuild + smoke test + push.

      155      return output

      157  
      158 +def _parse_timestamp(value) -> float:                         
      159 +    """Parse a timestamp expressed as float seconds or ``"HH:M
          +M:SS[.fraction]"``."""                                        
      160 +    if isinstance(value, (int, float)):                       
      161 +        return float(value)                                   
      162 +    text = str(value or "").strip()                           
      163 +    if not text:                                              
      164 +        raise ValueError("empty timestamp")                   
      165 +    if ":" in text:                                           
      166 +        parts = text.split(":")                               
      167 +        if len(parts) == 2:                                   
      168 +            minutes, seconds = parts                          
      169 +            return int(minutes) * 60 + float(seconds)         
      170 +        if len(parts) == 3:                                   
      171 +            hours, minutes, seconds = parts                   
      172 +            return int(hours) * 3600 + int(minutes) * 60 + flo
          +at(seconds)                                                   
      173 +        raise ValueError(f"unsupported timestamp format: {text
          +!r}")                                                         
      174 +    return float(text)                                        
      175 +                                                              
      176 +                                                              
      177 +def extract_video_screenshots(                                
      178 +    source_path: str | Path,                                  
      179 +    output_dir: str | Path,                                   
      180 +    *,                                                        
      181 +    count: int | None = None,                                 
      182 +    timestamps: list | tuple | None = None,                   
      183 +    seed: int = 0,                                            
      184 +    quality: int = 2,                                         
      185 +    runner=run_subprocess,                                    
      186 +    duration_reader=probe_video_duration,                     
      187 +    date_stamp: str | None = None,                            
      188 +) -> list[Path]:                                              
      189 +    """Extract still images from a video at given or random of
          +fsets.                                                        
      190 +                                                              
      191 +    The output filename uses the format                       
      192 +    ``{original_stem}_{YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS}_screenshot{N}.jpg`` wh
          +ere N is the                                                  
      193 +    1-based index of the screenshot in the resulting list.    
      194 +                                                              
      195 +    If ``timestamps`` is provided it overrides ``count`` and i
          +s taken as                                                    
      196 +    the explicit offsets (float seconds, or ``"HH:MM:SS"`` str
          +ings). Otherwise                                              
      197 +    ``count`` evenly-spaced offsets are placed inside the vide
          +o duration                                                    
      198 +    with deterministic jitter driven by ``seed`` so repeated e
          +xtractions                                                    
      199 +    on the same seed produce identical results.               
      200 +    """                                                       
      201 +    source = Path(source_path).expanduser().resolve()         
      202 +    out_dir = Path(output_dir).expanduser().resolve()         
      203 +    out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)                
      204 +                                                              
      205 +    if timestamps is not None:                                
      206 +        offsets = [_parse_timestamp(item) for item in timestam
          +ps]                                                           
      207 +    else:                                                     
      208 +        if not count or count < 1:                            
      209 +            raise ValueError("count must be >= 1 when timestam
          +ps is not provided")                                          
      210 +        duration = duration_reader(source, runner=runner)     
      211 +        if duration <= 0:                                     
      212 +            raise ValueError(f"video has non-positive duration
          +: {duration}")                                                
      213 +        rng = random.Random(seed)                             
      214 +        offsets = []                                          
      215 +        for index in range(count):                            
      216 +            # Distribute roughly evenly across the timeline, a
          +voiding the                                                   
      217 +            # very first and last 1% so we don't grab a blank 
          +frame.                                                        
      218 +            segment_start = duration * (index + 0.05) / count 
      219 +            segment_end = duration * (index + 0.95) / count   
      220 +            offsets.append(rng.uniform(segment_start, segment_
          +end))                                                         
      221 +                                                              
      222 +    if not offsets:                                           
      223 +        return []                                             
      224 +                                                              
      225 +    if date_stamp is None:                                    
      226 +        from datetime import datetime as _dt                  
      227 +        date_stamp = _dt.now().strftime("%Y%m%d-%H%M%S")      
      228 +                                                              
      229 +    stem = source.stem                                        
      230 +    results: list[Path] = []                                  
      231 +    for index, offset in enumerate(offsets, start=1):         
      232 +        output_path = out_dir / f"{stem}_{date_stamp}_screensh
          +ot{index}.jpg"                                                
      233 +        runner(                                               
      234 +            [                                                 
      235 +                FFMPEG_COMMAND,                               
      236 +                "-y",                                         
      237 +                "-ss",                                        
      238 +                f"{max(0.0, float(offset)):.3f}",             
      239 +                "-i",                                         
      240 +                str(source),                                  
      241 +                "-frames:v",                                  
      242 +                "1",                                          
      243 +                "-q:v",                                       
      244 +                str(int(quality)),                            
      245 +                str(output_path),                             
      246 +            ],                                                
      247 +            capture_output=True,                              
      248 +            text=True,                                        
      249 +        )                                                     
      250 +        results.append(output_path)                           
      251 +    return results                                            
      252 +                                                              
      253 +                                                              
      254  def extract_video_audio(
      255      source_path: str | Path,
      256      output_path: str | Path,

      56 +def _first_comment_text(payload: dict) -> str:                 
      57 +    """Return the trimmed first-comment text, or empty string."
         +""                                                             
      58 +    draft = payload.get("draft") or {}                         
      59 +    text = str(draft.get("firstComment") or payload.get("firstC
         +omment") or "").strip()                                        
      60 +    return text                                                
      61 +                                                               
      62 +                                                               
      63 +def _try_post_first_comment(                                   
      64 +    *,                                                         
      65 +    platform: str,                                             
      66 +    post_id: str | None,                                       
      67 +    text: str,                                                 
      68 +    poster,                                                    
      69 +    logger=None,                                               
      70 +) -> None:                                                     
      71 +    """Best-effort: post a follow-up comment via ``poster(post_
         +id, text)``.                                                   
      72 +                                                               
      73 +    A failure is logged but does not propagate, so a flaky comm
         +ents API                                                       
      74 +    cannot fail the main publish. ``poster`` must accept ``(pos
         +t_id, text)``                                                  
      75 +    and may return any value.                                  
      76 +    """                                                        
      77 +    if not (post_id and text):                                 
      78 +        return                                                 
      79 +    try:                                                       
      80 +        poster(post_id, text)                                  
      81 +    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001                   
      82 +        if logger is not None:                                 
      83 +            try:                                               
      84 +                logger("first_comment_failed", platform=platfor
         +m, post_id=post_id, error=str(exc))                            
      85 +            except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001                  
      86 +                pass                                           
      87 +        else:                                                  
      88 +            import logging as _logging                         
      89 +            _logging.getLogger(__name__).warning(              
      90 +                "first-comment post failed on %s for post %s: %
         +s",                                                            
      91 +                platform, post_id, exc,                        
      92 +            )                                                  
      93 +                                                               
      94 +                                                               
      95  def _get_session(session=None):
      96      if session is not None:
      97          return session

в—Ҹ Pushed to main as 3806202. Quick recap of what's live:

  New Publish Center UX (replaces the old multi-tab page):
  - Drag-drop upload accepting images & videos
  - Multi-select profile picker; account chips default to all enabled
  - Toggles: watermark, intro, outro, link-in-first-comment, screenshot count +
  timestamps
  - Brief textarea вҶ’ "Generate previews" вҶ’ per-account editable drafts with
  regenerate buttons
  - Schedule now or pick a start time
  - Load / save / manage templates (new sidebar entry зҜ„жң¬з®ЎзҗҶ)

  Backend additions:
  - extract_video_screenshots in media_pipeline.py with
  originalname_YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS_screenshotN.jpg naming
  - myUtils/platform_capabilities.py вҖ” single-source-of-truth for single-media
  platforms and first-comment support
  - myUtils/publish_orchestrator.py вҖ” fans out across profiles, applies the
  5-minute stagger when a single-media platform gets multiple files
  - myUtils/publish_templates.py + Alembic migration 0010 (templates table +
  campaign_posts.file_record_ids_json)
  - New endpoints: /publish-center/preview, /publish-center/regenerate,
  /publish-center/submit, /publish-templates[/<id>] CRUD
  - Facebook + Instagram first-comment posting after publish (guarded вҖ” failures
   log, never abort)
  - Worker filters artifacts by file_record_ids so staggered posts only carry
  their pinned media
  - Dockerfile installs ffmpeg so watermark/screenshot/concat actually work
  inside the container

  Smoke test in Docker: preview returns proper per-account draft structure,
  submit creates a campaign + enqueues a job, templates CRUD round-trips
  cleanly, frontend bundle contains the new endpoint paths, no errors in
  container logs.

  Not yet wired: Twitter & Reddit first-comment APIs (declared unsupported in
  SUPPORTS_FIRST_COMMENT for now so the orchestrator folds the link back into
  the body for those platforms); rclone is not installed in the image
  (orchestrator defaults uploadToRemote: false, so this is fine until a user
  opts in).

  silently falling back to file.name, dropping the uuid-prefixed path вҶ’ fixed to
   read the response data string.

  whole artifact prep, dropping the campaign вҶ’ wrapped in try/except so
  transcription is best-effort.

  silently failed вҶ’ added the same absolute-path resolution used for main media.

  templates

     Taiwan LGBTQIA+ Resources Page

     Context

     The user maintains the social-auto-upload project (Vue + Flask). Their
     request is unrelated to that tool's core function вҖ” they want to add a
     curated directory of ~21 Taiwanese LGBTQIA+ organizations to the app as a
     new Resources page. Each entry should carry the org's Chinese + English
     name, a 1вҖ“2 sentence mission intro, its services/focus areas, contact info
     (website / phone / email), any social-media presence we can verify, and a
     source URL citing where the intro came from.

     The project today has no resources/directory/links page of any kind вҖ” only
     the existing About page (sau_frontend/src/views/About.vue) which describes
     the tool itself. Per the user's choice, a new dedicated page is the right
     shape. The data is static once curated, so it lives as a frontend-only JSON
      file imported directly into the Vue component вҖ” no backend endpoint, no
     DB, no migration.

     в”ҳ

     ---
     Recommended Approach

     1. Data file вҖ” sau_frontend/src/data/lgbtqia-taiwan.json (new)

     A plain JSON array. Each entry follows this schema:

     {
       "id": "taiwan-equality-campaign",
       "nameZh": "еҸ°зҒЈеҪ©иҷ№е№іж¬ҠеӨ§е№іеҸ°еҚ”жңғ",
       "nameEn": "Taiwan Equality Campaign",
       "intro": "Founded 2016 as the Marriage Equality Coalition and renamed in
     2020; advocates for LGBTIQ+ rights through legislative work, political
     lobbying, public education, and international cooperation.",
       "services": ["Advocacy", "Public education", "Political lobbying",
     "International cooperation"],
       "website": "https://equallove.tw",
       "email": "equallovetw@equallove.tw",
       "phone": "(02) 4239-0254",
       "social": {
         "facebook": "https://www.facebook.com/equallovetw",
         "instagram": null,
         "linkedin": "https://www.linkedin.com/company/taiwan-equality-campaign"
       },
       "region": "Taipei",
       "source": "https://equallove.tw/en/about-us"
     }

     Fields omitted when unknown stay null so the UI can conditionally hide
     them. region is best-effort (used for filter chips on the page).

     2. New view вҖ” sau_frontend/src/views/Resources.vue (new)

     - Single-column responsive list of el-card entries.
     - Top: page title гҖҢLGBTQIA+ еҸӢе–„иіҮжәҗгҖҚ, short paragraph explaining this is
      a curated community directory.
     - Filter chip row: е…ЁйғЁ / Advocacy / Counselling / HIV+ Support / Education
      / Pride / Regional (filter by services and region).
     - Per-card layout:
       - Header: zh name (large) + en name (subtitle) + region tag.
       - Body: intro paragraph; services as el-tag chips.
       - Footer: website link (opens in new tab), phone, email, social icons; a
     small "иіҮж–ҷдҫҶжәҗ" link to source URL.
     - Empty state if no orgs match the filter.

     Component shape mirrors TemplateManagement.vue so it feels consistent.

     3. Router + sidebar вҖ” minimal changes

     - sau_frontend/src/router/index.js: import Resources and register
     /resources (Vue Router 4 hash mode like existing routes).
     - sau_frontend/src/App.vue: insert <el-menu-item index="/resources"> near
     the bottom of the sidebar with an icon like <Connection /> or <HelpFilled 
     /> and label иіҮжәҗйҖЈзөҗ (or гҖҢеҸӢе–„иіҮжәҗгҖҚ).

     4. Data collection (execution-time)

     During execution, search each org via the Brave вҶ’ Exa вҶ’ Tavily fallback
     chain (Brave is currently failing with SUBSCRIPTION_TOKEN_INVALID, so the
     first hop will skip straight to Exa). For each org, gather:

     - Canonical website (prefer official .org.tw / .tw domain).
     - A 1вҖ“2 sentence intro paraphrased from the official "About" or "й—ңж–јжҲ‘еҖ‘"
     page.
     - 3вҖ“5 service categories from the services / programs section.
     - Contact details listed on their site.
     - Verifiable social-media URLs (skip if not found).
     - Record the exact source URL used.

     Skip orgs where no verifiable official source can be found within ~3 search
      attempts вҖ” note them as intro: null, source: null so the page still lists
     them with a TODO marker rather than fabricating content.

     No backend / DB / migration touched.

     Reused Patterns

     - View / card layout patterns from
     sau_frontend/src/views/TemplateManagement.vue and About.vue.
     - Sidebar pattern in sau_frontend/src/App.vue:23-58.
     - Router pattern in sau_frontend/src/router/index.js.
     - @element-plus/icons-vue for the menu icon.

     Verification

     1. cd sau_frontend && npm run build вҖ” must complete with no errors.
     2. docker compose build social-auto-upload && docker compose up -d вҖ”
     container starts cleanly.
     3. Visit http://localhost:5409/#/resources in a browser:
       - Verify all 21 orgs render in cards.
       - Verify filter chips correctly hide/show entries.
       - Verify the "иіҮж–ҷдҫҶжәҗ" link for each card opens its source URL in a new
     tab.
       - Verify external website links also open in a new tab (target="_blank" 
     rel="noopener noreferrer").
     4. Sidebar entry иіҮжәҗйҖЈзөҗ is visible and selecting it navigates to
     /resources.
     5. Commit + push to GitHub once the page renders cleanly.

     Risks

     - Stale or wrong contact info: some smaller orgs (её•дёүе°ҸдәӢеӢҷжүҖ,
     еҚ—ж–№еҪ©иҷ№иЎ—6иҷҹ, еңӢз«Ӣй«ҳйӣ„её«зҜ„еӨ§еӯёжҖ§еҲҘж•ҷиӮІз ”з©¶жүҖеӯёжңғ) may not have rich web
     presence. Plan: include an intro: null marker rather than guess.
     - Brave search API key invalid: already verified вҖ” fall through to Exa
     (works) immediately, then Tavily if Exa rate-limits.
     - English translations of small orgs: leave nameEn: null when no official
     English name is on the org's site rather than invent one.

вқҜ and we still need API v2 because we need the insight right?? plan this as well and teach me how to give those value to Patreon for applying api v2. Hopefully it's free. if not then we don't need it 
в—Ҹ Plan written. Addressing the new question and updating the plan to fold
  Patreon insights into the Stats Dashboard section.

  Patreon API v2 вҖ” answers to your question:

  - You have no choice вҖ” it's v2 or nothing. Patreon explicitly says "Only API
  v2 is available for new clients. The version cannot be changed after
  creation." Your form has v2 pre-selected.
  - Yes, it's free. Patreon Platform API has no paid tier вҖ” no monthly fee, no
  per-call cost. Rate-limited (~ a few hundred req/min per token) but free.
  - "Applying for API v2" is just filling out the Create Client form you're 
  looking at. No separate review process. As soon as you click Create, Patreon
  issues a client_id + client_secret and you can start OAuth flows immediately.
  - Scopes are requested at OAuth time, not at client creation. The Create
  Client form doesn't ask you to pick scopes вҖ” you just enter the basics (name,
  redirect URI, etc.). When your backend builds the authorize URL, it appends
  scope=identity campaigns campaigns.posts (URL-encoded as
  identity%20campaigns%20campaigns.posts). The user sees those on the consent
  screen and approves them.
  - Scopes that don't need any special approval (auto-granted):
    - identity вҖ” user's name, profile pic, etc. (for the "Connected as @creator"
   badge)
    - campaigns вҖ” list the connected user's creator pages
    - campaigns.posts вҖ” read posts on the connected user's own campaign вҶ’ this
  is what gives you insights (like_count, comment_count per post, plus
  published_at / title)
    - On the campaign object itself: patron_count, pledge_sum (total $
  pledged/month), creation_count вҖ” these are returned with the campaigns scope,
  no extra ask.
  - Scopes that do need a review (skip unless we add a paid-membership feature
  later): campaigns.members[email], campaigns.members.address (these touch PII
  so Patreon vets them manually). We don't need these.

  Folding this into the plan now.

     Patreon Support + TikTok Re-Review Demo + Stats Dashboard

     Context

     Three parallel pieces of work, all in /home/will/social-auto-upload:

     1. Patreon support вҖ” the codebase already declares PLATFORM_PATREON
     (myUtils/profiles.py:51), routes the platform through
     _publish_prepared_not_implemented in myUtils/worker.py:595, has
     PlatformRule("patreon", long_form=True) in content_rules.py, and
     AccountManagement.vue:538-541, 751, 1072, 2327-2328 already exposes a
     patreonCampaignId field on the account form. Everything is stubbed for
     Patreon except: no Playwright uploader, no OAuth flow, no publisher
     implementation. User chose Playwright cookie automation (mirroring 9
     existing uploaders) because Patreon's public API v2 doesn't expose a
     post-creation endpoint.
     2. TikTok app re-review вҖ” reviewer asked for one demo video that exercises
     every declared product/scope (Login Kit + user.info.basic, Content Posting
     API + video.upload + video.publish, Webhooks) in the sandbox. New sandbox
     creds: sbawqxthixw67j7i7p / qfim5q2edKWWDbKEcshvu52FAY2ViPQG. Current
     production creds in .env: TIKTOK_CLIENT_KEY=awhwvswj145tzpry. Production
     callback https://socialupload.iamwillywang.com/oauth/tiktok/callback is
     already wired (sau_backend.py:3802,3842). The flow exists end-to-end; the
     script just needs to walk through it with sandbox creds.
     3. Stats dashboard вҖ” sau_frontend/src/views/Dashboard.vue (637 LOC) shows
     account counts only, no per-post analytics. publish_job_targets table has
     no column for the platform-side post id/url, so we can't yet pull metrics
     back. No chart library in sau_frontend/package.json. User wants TikTok +
     Meta + YouTube + Twitter (all four if any free tier supports them). Of
     those: TikTok Display API, Meta Page/IG Insights, YouTube Analytics are
     free; Twitter/X API v2 analytics is paid-only (Basic $100/mo) вҖ” I'll plan
     for the three free ones and note Twitter as a follow-up gated on tier
     upgrade.

     ---
     Part 1 вҖ” Quick Answers (no code)

     1A. Patreon "Create Client" form

     Note on API v2 / pricing: only v2 is available for new clients
     (auto-selected on the form). It is free вҖ” Patreon Platform API has no paid
     tier or per-call cost, just rate limits. Submitting the Create Client form
     is the application вҖ” Patreon issues client_id + client_secret immediately,
     no separate review. Scopes are not chosen on this form; they're appended to
      the OAuth authorize URL at runtime (see Part 2A). The scopes we will
     request (identity, campaigns, campaigns.posts) are auto-granted on user
     consent вҖ” none require Patreon's PII review.

     Field: App Name
     Value to enter: Socialupload вң“
     в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
     Field: Description
     Value to enter: Socialupload helps creators publish the same video or post 
     to 
       multiple platforms (Patreon, YouTube, TikTok, Instagram, Facebook, 
     Threads, 
       Reddit, Twitter, Bilibili and more) from one dashboard. With Patreon, 
     after a
        creator connects their account, Socialupload reads basic profile and 
       campaign info to confirm the right account is connected, and publishes 
     posts 
       that the creator composes inside Socialupload to the creator's selected 
       Patreon campaign. All publishing is user-initiated; we never post without
      
       explicit user action. (вүҲ 540 chars)

     Part 3 вҖ” Stats Dashboard

     3A. Schema migration 0011_post_metrics.py (new)

     op.add_column("publish_job_targets", sa.Column("platform_post_id", sa.Text,
      nullable=True))
     op.add_column("publish_job_targets", sa.Column("platform_post_url",
     sa.Text, nullable=True))
     op.add_column("publish_job_targets", sa.Column("metrics_json", sa.Text,
     nullable=True))
     op.add_column("publish_job_targets", sa.Column("metrics_fetched_at",
     sa.DateTime, nullable=True))
     op.create_index("idx_publish_job_targets_post_id", "publish_job_targets",
     ["platform_post_id"])

     3B. Capture post_id at publish time

     In myUtils/prepared_publishers.py each publish_*_sync returns an id today
     (FB id, IG publish.id, YouTube id, Twitter id, TikTok needs a follow-up
     /status/fetch call after publish completes). Plumb that id back to the
     worker, which writes it onto the target row. In
     myUtils/worker.py:_run_prepared_campaign_upload (line 599), catch the
     publisher's return value and call a new
     myUtils/jobs.py:set_target_post_identifiers(target_id, post_id, post_url).

     3C. Per-platform metrics fetcher вҖ” myUtils/insights/ (new module)

     File: myUtils/insights/tiktok.py
     Platform: TikTok
     API + scope: Display API /v2/research/video/query/ requires Research API
       approval вҖ” prefer the Content Posting API status endpoint
       /v2/post/publish/status/fetch/ for upload state, plus Display API
       /v2/video/list/ with new scope video.list (must be added to TikTok  app +

       re-reviewed)
     Metrics: view_count, like_count, comment_count, share_count

     File: myUtils/insights/patreon.py (new)
     Platform: Patreon
     API + scope: Patreon API v2 (free). GET 
       /api/oauth2/v2/campaigns/{id}?fields[campaign]=patron_count,pledge_sum,cr
     eation_count
        for campaign-level stats (patron count, total monthly pledge $, post
     count),
        and GET 
       /api/oauth2/v2/campaigns/{id}/posts?fields[post]=title,published_at,like_
     count,comment_count
        to fan out per-post engagement. Uses the access token already stored by
       myUtils/patreon_auth.py. Requires only scopes campaigns + campaigns.posts

       (auto-granted).
     Metrics: patrons, pledge_sum_usd, likes, comments per post

     Common signature: fetch_metrics(account, platform_post_id) -> dict
     returning a normalized {views, likes, comments, shares, impressions?, 
     reach?, fetched_at}.

     3D. Scheduled metric refresh

     A new background worker in myUtils/insights/refresher.py queries
     publish_job_targets WHERE status='succeeded' AND platform_post_id IS NOT 
     NULL AND (metrics_fetched_at IS NULL OR metrics_fetched_at < now - 
     interval) and updates metrics_json. Run on a configurable interval
     (SAU_METRICS_REFRESH_SECONDS, default 3600s, similar to the existing
     _account_maintenance_loop pattern at sau_backend.py:1979).

     ---
     Verification

     Patreon

     1. docker compose build && docker compose up -d
     2. Create a Patreon test account, configure PATREON_CLIENT_ID/SECRET in
     .env
     3. Add account in UI вҶ’ click Log in to Patreon (browser) вҶ’ Chromium opens,
     log in, cookie saved
     4. Click Connect with Patreon (OAuth) вҶ’ identity + campaign list populated
     5. Publish a test post from Publish Center вҶ’ confirm it appears as draft on
      the creator's Patreon dashboard
     6. Toggle "publish directly" and re-test
     7. Confirm worker logs show _publish_patreon_post not
     _publish_prepared_not_implemented

     TikTok demo video

     1. Swap .env to sandbox creds, restart container
     2. Record the 11-scene storyboard above
     3. Verify the video shows: domain in URL bar, OAuth consent showing all
     three scopes, draft mode + direct-post mode + confirmation modal, webhook
     events list
     4. Revert .env to production, restart, upload mp4 to the App Review form
     with the existing description

     Stats

     1. Run alembic upgrade head вҖ” verify platform_post_id / metrics_json
     columns appear on publish_job_targets
     2. Publish a post to each platform and confirm platform_post_id is captured
      (check via sqlite3 db/database.db "SELECT platform, platform_post_id, 
     platform_post_url FROM publish_job_targets ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10")
     3. Trigger the refresher manually (python -c "from 
     myUtils.insights.refresher import refresh_once; refresh_once()"); verify
     metrics_json populated for each
     4. For Patreon: connect a creator account, publish a post via the cookie
     uploader, wait for the refresher to populate like_count / comment_count
     from /campaigns/{id}/posts вҖ” and the Stats page shows the campaign-level
     patron_count + pledge_sum
     5. Visit /#/stats in the browser; verify the four platform tiles + per-post
      table render with real numbers
     6. Edge: confirm Twitter cards show a "API tier upgrade required"
     placeholder rather than crashing

     Risks / Notes

     - Patreon UI selectors are unstable. Patreon's post editor is a heavy React
      app; selectors drift. Mitigate with data-testid discovery + a fallback
     wait_for_selector chain like Medium's uploader does.
     - TikTok app re-review can take a week+ after re-submission. Schedule the
     video record at a low-traffic time so production isn't running sandbox
     creds for long.
     - Adding yt-analytics.readonly and instagram_manage_insights requires
     re-authorising existing connected accounts. Plan to surface a banner
     "Re-connect your YouTube account to enable analytics" rather than silently
     breaking.
     - Twitter analytics: deferred. The fetcher exists but is no-op on free tier
      вҖ” clearly documented.
